#rework
TUR_remove_add_dynamic_modifiers = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_national_economy } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_national_economy }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_national_economy }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_agrarian_economy } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_agrarian_economy }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_agrarian_economy }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_second_constitutional_era } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_second_constitutional_era }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_second_constitutional_era }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_a_bygone_era } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_a_bygone_era }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_a_bygone_era }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_the_modern_era } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_the_modern_era }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_army_of_the_modern_era }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_donanma_i_humayun } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_donanma_i_humayun }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_donanma_i_humayun }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_havacilik_komisyonu } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_havacilik_komisyonu }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_havacilik_komisyonu }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_sublime_realm } }
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_sublime_realm }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_sublime_realm }
		}
	}
}

TUR_add_appropriate_grand_vizier_for_bop = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_mahmud_sevket } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_mahmud_sevket
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_said_halim } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_said_halim
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_nazim_pasha } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_nazim_pasha
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ibrahim_hakki } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_ibrahim_hakki
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ali_fuat_turkgeldi } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_ali_fuat_turkgeldi
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ahmet_riza } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_ahmet_riza
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_huseyin_hilmi_pasha } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_huseyin_hilmi_pasha
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = TUR_ahmet_izzet } }
			set_power_balance = {
				id = TUR_government_committee_struggle
				right_side = TUR_government_committee_struggle_ahmet_izzet
			}
		}
	}
}

TUR_remove_current_sultan = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = HJZ_hussein_bin_ali }
		remove_ideas = HJZ_hussein_bin_ali
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_HJZ_hussein_bin_ali
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_mehmed_V }
		remove_ideas = TUR_mehmed_V
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_V
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_yusuf_izzettin }
		remove_ideas = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_yusuf_izzettin
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_mehmed_VI }
		remove_ideas = TUR_mehmed_VI
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_VI
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_abdulmecid_II }
		remove_ideas = TUR_abdulmecid_II
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_abdulmecid_II
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_ahmed_nihad }
		remove_ideas = TUR_ahmed_nihad
		set_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_ahmed_nihad
	}
}

TUR_add_current_sultan = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_HJZ_hussein_bin_ali }
		add_ideas = HJZ_hussein_bin_ali
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_V }
		add_ideas = TUR_mehmed_V
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_yusuf_izzettin }
		add_ideas = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_VI }
		add_ideas = TUR_mehmed_VI
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_abdulmecid_II }
		add_ideas = TUR_abdulmecid_II
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_ahmed_nihad }
		add_ideas = TUR_ahmed_nihad
	}
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_HJZ_hussein_bin_ali
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_V
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_yusuf_izzettin
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_mehmed_VI
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_abdulmecid_II
	clr_country_flag = TUR_had_TUR_ahmed_nihad
}

TUR_promote_officers_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_character = TUR_suleyman_faik
			TUR_suleyman_faik = { is_unit_leader = no } #1.1.1913
		}
		add_corps_commander_role = {
			character = TUR_suleyman_faik
			traits = { trait_engineer cavalry_leader career_officer }
			skill = 2
			attack_skill = 1
			defense_skill = 2
			planning_skill = 3
			logistics_skill = 2
		}
		TUR_suleyman_faik = { set_character_name = TUR_suleyman_faik_pasha }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {

			skill = 3

		}

			skill = 2
			attack_skill = 1
			defense_skill = 3
			planning_skill = 3
			logistics_skill = 2
		}
		TUR_selahattin_adil = { set_character_name = TUR_selahattin_adil_pasha }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_character = TUR_kazim_orbay
			TUR_kazim_orbay = { is_unit_leader = no } #31.8.1922
		}
		add_corps_commander_role = {
			character = TUR_kazim_orbay
			traits = { media_personality politically_connected infantry_leader }
			skill = 2
			attack_skill = 2
			defense_skill = 3
			planning_skill = 3
           logistics_skill = 2
		}
		TUR_kazim_orbay = { set_character_name = TUR_kazim_orbay_pasha }
	}
}

TUR_minority_revolt_effect = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = TUR
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					resistance > 79.9
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { resistance > 79.9 }
				controller = { country_event = ottoman.0 }
			}
		}
	}
}

TUR_reduce_armenian_level = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level < 2 } }
		remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_armenian_minority }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian
			min = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian
			min = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { state = 352 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.101 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 806 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.103 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 1022 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.134 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 881 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.135 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 355 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.136 days = 4 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { state = 1025 }
				ROOT = { country_event = { id = ottoman.135 days = 4 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_core_of = ARM }
			remove_core_of = ARM
			if = {
				limit = { state = 353 }
				354 = { remove_claim_by = ARM }
				1034 = { remove_claim_by = ARM }
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_modify_armenian_minority
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_attrition_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_attrition_armenian
			min = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_army_defence_factor_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_army_defence_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_enemy_local_supplies_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian = -0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_enemy_local_supplies_armenian
			max = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_minority_recruitable_population_armenian_down
		add_to_variable = { TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian = 0.05 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = TUR_ottoman_recruitable_population_factor_armenian
			max = 0
		}
	}
	add_to_variable = { TUR_armenian_state_level = -1 }
}

TUR_domestic_weapon_research_tank = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_domestic_weapon_companies
				has_completed_focus = TRS_domestic_weapon_companies
			}
			has_idea = tulomsas
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = TRS
				check_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_attack_factor < 0 }
				check_variable = { TUR_aoabe_army_defence_factor < 0 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TRS_domestic_weapon_research_tt
			add_to_variable = { TUR_o4a_army_attack_factor = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_o4a_army_attack_factor = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_o4a_army_attack_factor_tt = -0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_o4a_army_attack_factor_tt = -0.005 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

		every_state = {
			limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority } }
			set_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_variable = ROOT.TUR_greek_population_factor }
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level > 0 } }
				set_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_variable = ROOT.TUR_orthodox_population_factor }
				multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_variable = TUR_greek_orthodox_state_level }
				divide_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_orthodox_variable = 100 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_variable = TUR_greek_orthodox_variable }
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_variable = TUR_greek_state_level }
			divide_temp_variable = { TUR_greek_variable = 5 }
			set_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor = TUR_greek_variable }
			set_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor = TUR_greek_variable }
			#set_variable = { TUR_greek_population_political_power_factor = TUR_greek_variable }
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_greek_population_stability_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_political_power_factor > -0.001 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_greek_population_political_power_factor = 0 } }
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = TUR_greek_population_political_power_factor max = -0.001 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_ottoman_syria } }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_stability_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_war_support_factor = 3 }
				multiply_variable = { TUR_greek_population_political_power_factor = 3 }
			}
		}

			set_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10_opposite = 0.10 }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10 = -0.10 } }
			ROOT = { add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10_opposite = 0.10 } }
		}
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10 = TUR_has_debt_10_1 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10 = TUR_has_debt_10_2 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10 = TUR_has_debt_10_3 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10 = TUR_has_debt_10_4 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10 = TUR_has_debt_10_5 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10 = TUR_has_debt_10_6 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10 = TUR_has_debt_10_7 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10 = TUR_has_debt_10_8 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10 = TUR_has_debt_10_9 }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10_opposite = TUR_has_debt_10_1_opposite }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10_opposite = TUR_has_debt_10_2_opposite }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10_opposite = TUR_has_debt_10_3_opposite }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10_opposite = TUR_has_debt_10_4_opposite }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10_opposite = TUR_has_debt_10_5_opposite }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10_opposite = TUR_has_debt_10_6_opposite }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10_opposite = TUR_has_debt_10_7_opposite }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10_opposite = TUR_has_debt_10_8_opposite }
		add_to_variable = { TUR_has_debt_10_opposite = TUR_has_debt_10_9_opposite }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPD_idea }
			remove_ideas = TUR_OPD_idea
			add_ideas = TUR_OPD_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPD_idea_2 }
			remove_ideas = TUR_OPD_idea_2
			add_ideas = TUR_OPD_idea_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TUR_OPD_idea_3 }
			remove_ideas = TUR_OPD_idea_3
			add_ideas = TUR_OPD_idea_3
		}
	}
}

TUR_remove_debt_1_FROM = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_1
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.01 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_FROM
		}
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.01 }
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = 0.01 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods
			min = 0
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
			max = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.01 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_FROM
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_1_FROM }
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = 0.01 }
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = -0.01 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods
					max = 0
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
					min = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_debt_value_check = yes
}

TUR_remove_debt_2_FROM = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_2
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.02 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_FROM
		}

		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = 0.02 }

			var = opda_consumer_goods
			min = 0
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
			max = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { FROM = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.02 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_FROM
		}

			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_ENG
		}
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.03 }
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = 0.03 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods
			min = 0
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
			max = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { ENG = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		if = {
			limit = { ENG = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.03 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_ENG
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_3_ENG }

		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_85
		if = {
			limit = { AUS = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.85 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_AUS
		}
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = -0.85 }
		add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = 0.85 }
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods
			min = 0
		}
		clamp_variable = {
			var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
			max = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { AUS = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
		if = {
			limit = { AUS = { check_variable = { opda_consumer_goods > -0.85 } } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_AUS
		}
		else = { custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_85_AUS }
		hidden_effect = {
			AUS = {
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = 0.85 }
				add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = -0.85 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods
					max = 0
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
					min = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_debt_value_check = yes
}

TUR_investment_add_effect = {
	effect_tooltip = {
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = FRA } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_FRA
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_ENG
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_GER
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = BEL } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_BEL
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = HOL } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_HOL
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = ITA } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_ITA
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = AUS } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_AUS
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = USA } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_USA
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = RUS } }
			activate_mission = TUR_investments_from_RUS
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_investment_add_effect_tt
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_infrastructure } }
			var:FROM.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = FRA } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_FRA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_ENG = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_GER = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = BEL } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_BEL = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = HOL } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_HOL = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = ITA } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_ITA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = AUS } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_AUS = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = RUS } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_RUS = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = USA } }
				TUR_add_debt_5_USA = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_consumer } }
			var:FROM.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = FRA } }
				TUR_add_debt_8_FRA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
				TUR_add_debt_8_ENG = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
				TUR_add_debt_8_GER = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = BEL } }
				TUR_add_debt_8_BEL = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = HOL } }
				TUR_add_debt_8_HOL = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = ITA } }
				TUR_add_debt_8_ITA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = AUS } }
				TUR_add_debt_8_AUS = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = RUS } }
				TUR_add_debt_8_RUS = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = USA } }
				TUR_add_debt_8_USA = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_military
						has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_military } }
				var:FROM.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = arms_factory
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { has_country_flag = already_investing_in_the_ottomans_dockyard } }
				var:FROM.ottoman_investment_targeted_state = {
					add_building_construction = {
						type = dockyard
						level = 1
						instant_build = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = FRA } }
				TUR_add_debt_10_FRA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
				TUR_add_debt_10_ENG = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
				TUR_add_debt_10_GER = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = BEL } }
				TUR_add_debt_10_BEL = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = HOL } }
				TUR_add_debt_10_HOL = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = ITA } }
				TUR_add_debt_10_ITA = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = AUS } }
				TUR_add_debt_10_AUS = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = RUS } }
				TUR_add_debt_10_RUS = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tag = USA } }
				TUR_add_debt_10_USA = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_idea = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
			FROM = { remove_ideas = TUR_minimal_investment_in_the_ottomans }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_idea = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
			FROM = { remove_ideas = TUR_moderate_investment_in_the_ottomans }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_idea = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans } }
			FROM = { remove_ideas = TUR_large_investment_in_the_ottomans }
		}
	}
}

TUR_anatolian_grain_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain
			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_2
		}
	}

		swap_ideas = {

			add_idea = TUR_anatolian_grain_3
		}

TUR_reduce_naval_blockade = {
	add_to_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade = -1 }
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_naval_blockade }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade > 1 } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_naval_blockade_reduce_1
			add_to_variable = { TUR_nb_monthly_population = -0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_nb_consumer_goods_factor  = 0.005 }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_nb_war_stability_factor = -0.01 }
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade
				add_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { TUR_naval_blockade < 2 } }
			remove_ideas = TUR_naval_blockade
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { global.TUR_reduce_naval_blockade_naval_blockade = TUR_naval_blockade }
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_idea = TUR_great_famine_of_syria }
				country_event = { id = ottoman.161 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
	}
}

increase_state_development_category = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = wasteland }
		set_state_category = pastoral
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = enclave }
		set_state_category = pastoral
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = tiny_island }
		set_state_category = small_island
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = pastoral }
		set_state_category = rural
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = small_island }
		set_state_category = rural
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = rural }
		set_state_category = town
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = town }
		set_state_category = large_town
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = large_town }
		set_state_category = city
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = city }
		set_state_category = large_city
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = large_city }
		set_state_category = metropolis
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_state_category = metropolis }
		set_state_category = megalopolis
	}
}

TUR_government_stability_calculate = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var > TUR_government_stability_max } }
		set_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var = TUR_government_stability_max }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var < 0 } }
		set_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_leader_with_trait = TUR_the_victorious
			check_variable = { TUR_government_stability_var < 50 }
		}
		country_event = ottoman.9
	}
}
TUR_government_popularity_calculate = {
	hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = { TUR_neutrality_popularity = party_popularity@neutrality }
		set_variable = { TUR_democratic_popularity = party_popularity@democratic }
		set_variable = { TUR_fascism_popularity = party_popularity@fascism }
		set_variable = { TUR_communism_popularity = party_popularity@communism }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_neutrality_itf
				has_country_flag = TUR_fascism_itf
			}
			add_to_variable = { TUR_neutrality_popularity = party_popularity@fascism }
			add_to_variable = { TUR_fascism_popularity = party_popularity@neutrality }
		}
	}
}

TUR_depoliticize_army_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_depoliticize_army_effect_1
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_1
				add_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_2
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_depoliticize_army_effect_2
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_2
				add_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_3
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_3 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_secure_officer_loyalty
					has_completed_focus = TUR_consolidate_military_positions
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_depoliticize_army_effect_3
			hidden_effect = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_3
					add_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_4
				}
			}
		}
		else = { remove_ideas = TUR_army_factionalism_3 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_4 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_secure_officer_loyalty
					has_completed_focus = TUR_consolidate_military_positions
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_depoliticize_army_effect_ittihadist_1
			hidden_effect = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_4
					add_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_ittihadist_2
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { always = no }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_depoliticize_army_effect_itilafist_1
			hidden_effect = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_4
					add_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_itilafist_2
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_ittihadist_2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_depoliticize_army_effect_ittihadist_2
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_ittihadist_2
				add_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_ittihadist_3
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_itilafist_2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_depoliticize_army_effect_itilafist_2
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_itilafist_2
				add_idea = TUR_army_factionalism_itilafist_3
			}
		}
	}
	TUR_government_stability_calculate = yes
}

		}
	}

TUR_liberation_war_defeat_effect = { #rework
	FROM = { white_peace = ROOT }
	if = {
		limit = {
			ENG = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
		}
		ENG = { puppet = TUR }
	}
	set_cosmetic_tag = TUR_Sultanate
	if = {
		limit = {
			GRE = { has_completed_focus = GRE_venizelos_tittoni_agreement }
			ITA = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
		}
		824 = { transfer_state_to = ITA }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			SOV = {
				exists = no
			}
			RUS = {
				exists = yes
				has_country_flag = great_war_winner
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			transfer_state = 352
			transfer_state = 353
			transfer_state = 806
		}
		else = {
			ARM = {
				transfer_state = 352
				transfer_state = 353
				transfer_state = 806
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			GRE = { has_country_flag = pontus_rebellion }
		}
		PON = {
			transfer_state = 354
			transfer_state = 1034
			transfer_state = 355
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ARM = {
						owns_state = 353
					}
				}
				transfer_state = 354
				transfer_state = 1034
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			GRE = {
				has_country_flag = pontus_confederation
			}
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		ARM = {
			annex_country = {
				target = PON
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PON
				}
				remove_core_of = PON
				add_core_of = ARM
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = PONARM
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			FRA = { has_country_flag = great_war_winner }
		}
		TUR = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 344
						state = 857
						state = 829
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = FRA
			}					
		}
	}
	release = KUR
}

TRS_increase_arab_opposition = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_0 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TRS_arab_opposition_increase_1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_0
				add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_1
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TRS_arab_opposition_increase_2_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_1
				add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_2
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_2 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = TRS_arab_opposition_increase_1_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_2
				add_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_3
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_3 }

TRS_remove_arab_opposition = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_arab_opposition_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_0 }
			remove_ideas = TRS_arab_opposition_0
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_1 }
			remove_ideas = TRS_arab_opposition_1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_2 }
			remove_ideas = TRS_arab_opposition_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_3 }
			remove_ideas = TRS_arab_opposition_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_4 }
			remove_ideas = TRS_arab_opposition_4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_5 }
			remove_ideas = TRS_arab_opposition_5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_6 }
			remove_ideas = TRS_arab_opposition_6
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_7 }
			remove_ideas = TRS_arab_opposition_7
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_8 }
			remove_ideas = TRS_arab_opposition_8
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRS_arab_opposition_9 }
			remove_ideas = TRS_arab_opposition_9
		}
	}
